## åã€äº‹ä»¶ç»‘å®šæŒ‡ä»¤

ä½¿ç”¨Vueæ—¶ï¼Œå¦‚éœ€ä¸ºDOMæ³¨å†Œäº‹ä»¶ï¼ŒåŠå…¶çš„ç®€å•ï¼Œè¯­æ³•å¦‚ä¸‹ï¼š

- \<button v-on:äº‹ä»¶å="å†…è”è¯­å¥">æŒ‰é’®\</button>
- \<button v-on:äº‹ä»¶å="å¤„ç†å‡½æ•°">æŒ‰é’®\</button>
- \<button v-on:äº‹ä»¶å="å¤„ç†å‡½æ•°(å®å‚)">æŒ‰é’®\</button>
- `v-on:` ç®€å†™ä¸º **@**

1. å†…è”è¯­å¥

```vue

    <button @click="count--">-</button>
    <span>{{ count }}</span>

    const app = new Vue({
        el: '#app',
        data: {
            count: 100
        }
    })
</script>
```

2. äº‹ä»¶å¤„ç†å‡½æ•°

   æ³¨æ„ï¼š
    - äº‹ä»¶å¤„ç†å‡½æ•°åº”è¯¥å†™åˆ°ä¸€ä¸ªè·ŸdataåŒçº§çš„é…ç½®é¡¹ï¼ˆmethodsï¼‰ä¸­
    - methodsä¸­çš„å‡½æ•°å†…éƒ¨çš„thiséƒ½æŒ‡å‘Vueå®ä¾‹

```vue

    <button @click="change">åˆ‡æ¢æ˜¾ç¤ºéšè—</button>
    <h1 v-show="isShow">é»‘é©¬ç¨‹åºå‘˜</h1>
</div>

<script>
    const app = new Vue({
        el: '#app',
        data: {
            isShow: true
        },
        methods: {
            change() {
                this.isShow = !this.isShow
            }
        }
    })
</script>
```

3. ç»™äº‹ä»¶å¤„ç†å‡½æ•°ä¼ å‚

- å¦‚æœä¸ä¼ é€’ä»»ä½•å‚æ•°ï¼Œåˆ™æ–¹æ³•æ— éœ€åŠ å°æ‹¬å·ï¼›methodsæ–¹æ³•ä¸­å¯ä»¥ç›´æ¥ä½¿ç”¨ e å½“åšäº‹ä»¶å¯¹è±¡
- å¦‚æœä¼ é€’äº†å‚æ•°ï¼Œåˆ™å®å‚ `$event` è¡¨ç¤ºäº‹ä»¶å¯¹è±¡ï¼Œå›ºå®šç”¨æ³•ã€‚

```vue

        border: 3px solid #000000;
        border-radius: 10px;
        padding: 20px;
        margin: 20px;
        width: 200px;
    }

    h3 {
        margin: 10px 0 20px 0;
    }

    p {
        margin: 20px;
    }

<div id="app">
    <div class="box">
        <h3>å°é»‘è‡ªåŠ¨å”®è´§æœº</h3>
        <button @click="buy(5, $event)">å¯ä¹5å…ƒ</button>
        <button @click="buy(10, $event)">å’–å•¡10å…ƒ</button>
        <button @click="buy(8, $event)">ç‰›å¥¶8å…ƒ</button>
    </div>
    <p>é“¶è¡Œå¡ä½™é¢ï¼š{{ money }}å…ƒ</p>
</div>

<script>
    const app = new Vue({
        el: '#app',
        data: {
            money: 1000
        },
        methods: {
            buy(n, $event) {
                this.money -= n
                console.log($event)
            }
        }
    })
</script>
```

## åä¸€ã€å±æ€§ç»‘å®šæŒ‡ä»¤

1. ä½œç”¨ï¼šåŠ¨æ€è®¾ç½®htmlçš„æ ‡ç­¾å±æ€§ æ¯”å¦‚ï¼šsrcã€urlã€title
2. è¯­æ³•ï¼šv-bind:å±æ€§å=â€œè¡¨è¾¾å¼â€
3. v-bindï¼šå¯ä»¥ç®€å†™æˆ => :

æ¯”å¦‚ï¼Œæœ‰ä¸€ä¸ªå›¾ç‰‡ï¼Œå®ƒçš„ `src` å±æ€§å€¼ï¼Œæ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªå›¾ç‰‡åœ°å€ã€‚è¿™ä¸ªåœ°å€åœ¨æ•°æ® data ä¸­å­˜å‚¨ã€‚

```vue

</div>

        el: '#app',
        data: {
            imgUrl: './imgs/10-02.png',
            msg: 'hello æ³¢ä»”'
        }
    })
```

## åäºŒã€å°æ¡ˆä¾‹-æ³¢ä»”çš„å­¦ä¹ ä¹‹æ—…

1. æ•°ç»„å­˜å‚¨å›¾ç‰‡è·¯å¾„ ['url1','url2','url3'ï¼Œ...]

```vue

                this.index += n

                return this.list[this.index]
            }
```

### 3.ç¿»è¯‘æ¡ˆä¾‹

```vue

<div id="app">
    <!-- æ¡ä»¶é€‰æ‹©æ¡† -->
    <div class="query">
        <span>ç¿»è¯‘æˆçš„è¯­è¨€ï¼š</span>
        <select>
            <option value="italy">æ„å¤§åˆ©</option>
            <option value="english">è‹±è¯­</option>
            <option value="german">å¾·è¯­</option>
        </select>
    </div>

    <div class="box">
        <div class="input-wrap">
            <textarea v-model="words"></textarea>
            <span><i>âŒ¨ï¸</i>æ–‡æ¡£ç¿»è¯‘</span>
        </div>
        <div class="output-wrap">
            <div class="transbox">{{ result }}</div>
        </div>

<script>

    const app = new Vue({
        el: '#app',
        data: {
            words: '',
            timer: null,
            result: ''
        },
        watch: {
            words(newValue) {
                if (this.timer) {
                    clearTimeout(this.timer)
                }
                this.timer = setTimeout(async () => {
                    const res = await axios({
                        url: 'https://applet-base-api-t.itheima.net/api/translate',
                        params: {
                            words: newValue
                        }
                    })

                    this.result = res.data.data
                }, 300)
            }
        }
    })
</script>
```

## äºŒå…«ã€watchä¾¦å¬å™¨

```vue
    }
```

```vue
        font-size: 20px;
        font-style: normal;
    }
</style>

<div id="app">
    <!-- æ¡ä»¶é€‰æ‹©æ¡† -->
    <div class="query">
        <span>ç¿»è¯‘æˆçš„è¯­è¨€ï¼š</span>
        <select v-model="item.lang">
            <option value="italy">æ„å¤§åˆ©</option>
            <option value="english">è‹±è¯­</option>
            <option value="german">å¾·è¯­</option>
        </select>
    </div>

    <!-- ç¿»è¯‘æ¡† -->
    <div class="box">
        <div class="input-wrap">
            <textarea v-model="item.words"></textarea>
            <span><i>âŒ¨ï¸</i>æ–‡æ¡£ç¿»è¯‘</span>
        </div>
        <div class="output-wrap">
            <div class="transbox">{{ result }}</div>

    </div>

<script>

    const app = new Vue({
        el: '#app',
        data: {
            item: {
                words: '',
                lang: 'italy'
            },
            timer: null,
            result: '',

        },
        watch: {
            item: {
                handler(newValue) {
                    if (this.timer) {
                        clearTimeout(this.timer)
                    }
                    this.timer = setTimeout(async () => {
                        const res = await axios({
                            url: 'https://applet-base-api-t.itheima.net/api/translate',
                            params: {
                                words: newValue
                            }
                        })

                        this.result = res.data.data
                    }, 300)
                },
                deep: true
            },
        }
    })
</script>
```

### 2.éœ€æ±‚åˆ†æ

### 3.æ€è·¯åˆ†æ

   - ç«‹åˆ»å‘é€è¯·æ±‚è·å–æ•°æ® created

   - ç»“åˆæ•°æ®ï¼Œè¿›è¡Œæ¸²æŸ“ v-for
   - æ¶ˆè´¹ç»Ÿè®¡  â€”> è®¡ç®—å±æ€§

   - æ”¶é›†è¡¨å•æ•°æ® v-modelï¼Œä½¿ç”¨æŒ‡ä»¤ä¿®é¥°ç¬¦å¤„ç†æ•°æ®
   - ç»™æ·»åŠ æŒ‰é’®æ³¨å†Œç‚¹å‡»äº‹ä»¶ï¼Œå¯¹è¾“å…¥çš„å†…å®¹åšéç©ºåˆ¤æ–­ï¼Œå‘é€è¯·æ±‚

4. é¥¼å›¾æ¸²æŸ“

   - æ ¹æ®æ•°æ®è¯•è¯•æ›´æ–°é¥¼å›¾ echarts.setOptions({...})

### 4.ä»£ç å‡†å¤‡

```vue
<div id="app">
    <div class="contain">
        <!-- å·¦ä¾§åˆ—è¡¨ -->
        <div class="list-box">

            <!-- æ·»åŠ èµ„äº§ -->
            <form class="my-form">
                <input type="text" class="form-control" placeholder="æ¶ˆè´¹åç§°" v-model.trim="name"/>
                <input type="text" class="form-control" placeholder="æ¶ˆè´¹ä»·æ ¼" v-model.number="price"/>
                <button type="button" class="btn btn-primary" @click="add">æ·»åŠ è´¦å•</button>
            </form>

            <table class="table table-hover">
                <thead>
                    <tr>
                        <th>ç¼–å·</th>
                        <th>æ¶ˆè´¹åç§°</th>
                        <th>æ¶ˆè´¹ä»·æ ¼</th>
                        <th>æ“ä½œ</th>
                    </tr>
                </thead>
                <tbody>
                    <tr v-for="(item, index) in list" :key="item.id">
                        <td>{{ index + 1 }}</td>
                        <td>{{ item.name }}</td>
                        <td :class="{ red: item.price > 500 }">{{ item.price.toFixed(2) }}</td>
                        <td><a href="javascript:;" @click="del(item.id)">åˆ é™¤</a></td>
                    </tr>
                </tbody>
                <tfoot>
                    <tr>
                        <td colspan="4">æ¶ˆè´¹æ€»è®¡ï¼š{{ totalPrice.toFixed(2) }}</td>
                    </tr>
                </tfoot>
            </table>
        </div>

        <!-- å³ä¾§å›¾è¡¨ -->
        <div class="echarts-box" id="main"></div>
    </div>
</div>

<script>
    /**
     * æ¥å£æ–‡æ¡£åœ°å€ï¼š
     * https://www.apifox.cn/apidoc/shared-24459455-ebb1-4fdc-8df8-0aff8dc317a8/api-53371058
     *
     * åŠŸèƒ½éœ€æ±‚ï¼š
     * 1. åŸºæœ¬æ¸²æŸ“
     * 2. æ·»åŠ åŠŸèƒ½
     * 3. åˆ é™¤åŠŸèƒ½
     * 4. é¥¼å›¾æ¸²æŸ“
     */
    const app = new Vue({
        el: '#app',
        data: {
            list: [],
            name: '',
            price: null
        },
        computed: {
            totalPrice() {
                return this.list.reduce((p, c) => p + c.price, 0)
            }
        },
        async created() {
            await this.getList()
        },
        methods: {
            async getList() {
                const res = await axios.get('https://applet-base-api-t.itheima.net/bill', {
                    params: {
                        creator: 'å°é»‘'
                    }
                })
                this.list = res.data.data

                this.myCharts.setOption({
                    series: [
                        {
                            data: this.list.map(ie => ({name: ie.name, value: ie.price}))
                        }
                    ]
                })
            },
            async add() {
                if (!this.name) {
                    return alert('è¯·è¾“å…¥æ¶ˆè´¹åç§°')
                }

                if (typeof this.price !== 'number') {
                    return alert('è¯·è¾“å…¥æ­£ç¡®çš„æ¶ˆè´¹åç§°')
                }

                await axios.post('https://applet-base-api-t.itheima.net/bill', {
                    creator: 'å°é»‘',
                    name: this.name,
                    price: this.price
                })

                this.getList()
                this.name = ''
                this.price = null
            },
            async del(id) {
                await axios.delete(`https://applet-base-api-t.itheima.net/bill/${id}`)

                this.getList()
            }
        },
        async mounted() {
            this.myCharts = echarts.init(document.querySelector('#main'))

            this.myCharts.setOption({
                title: {
                    text: 'æ¶ˆè´¹è´¦å•åˆ—è¡¨',
                    left: 'center'
                },
                tooltip: {
                    trigger: 'item'
                },
                legend: {
                    orient: 'vertical',
                    left: 'left'
                },
                series: [
                    {
                        name: 'æ¶ˆè´¹è´¦å•',
                        type: 'pie',
                        radius: '50%',
                        data: [],
                        emphasis: {
                            itemStyle: {
                                shadowBlur: 10,
                                shadowOffsetX: 0,
                                shadowColor: 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.5)'
                            }
                        }
                    }
                ]
            })
        }
    })
</script>
```

## ä¸‰å…«ã€æ™®é€šç»„ä»¶çš„æ³¨å†Œä½¿ç”¨-å±€éƒ¨æ³¨å†Œ

### 4.æ³¨æ„ï¼š

### 7.å­å‘çˆ¶é€šä¿¡ä»£ç ç¤ºä¾‹

å­ç»„ä»¶åˆ©ç”¨ **$emit** é€šçŸ¥çˆ¶ç»„ä»¶ï¼Œè¿›è¡Œä¿®æ”¹æ›´æ–°

```vue
</style>
```

## å››å…­ã€propsæ ¡éªŒå®Œæ•´å†™æ³•

### 1.è¯­æ³•

```vue

    æ ¡éªŒçš„å±æ€§å: {
        type: ç±»å‹, // Number String Boolean ...
        required: true, // æ˜¯å¦å¿…å¡«
        default: é»˜è®¤å€¼, // é»˜è®¤å€¼
        validator(value) {
            // è‡ªå®šä¹‰æ ¡éªŒé€»è¾‘
            return æ˜¯å¦é€šè¿‡æ ¡éªŒ
        }
    }

```

### 2.ä»£ç å®ä¾‹

```vue
        // å®Œæ•´å†™æ³•ï¼ˆç±»å‹ã€é»˜è®¤å€¼ã€éç©ºã€è‡ªå®šä¹‰æ ¡éªŒï¼‰
        props: {
            w: {
                type: Number,
                //required: true,
                default: 0,
                validator(val) {
                    // console.log(val)

                        console.error('ä¼ å…¥çš„èŒƒå›´å¿…é¡»æ˜¯0-100ä¹‹é—´')

                        return true
```

### 3.æ³¨æ„

## å››ä¹ã€éçˆ¶å­é€šä¿¡-event bus äº‹ä»¶æ€»çº¿

## äº”ä¸€ã€v-modelåŸç†

### 1.åŸç†ï¼š

v-modelæœ¬è´¨ä¸Šæ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªè¯­æ³•ç³–ã€‚ä¾‹å¦‚åº”ç”¨åœ¨è¾“å…¥æ¡†ä¸Šï¼Œå°±æ˜¯ value å±æ€§å’Œ input äº‹ä»¶çš„åˆå†™


### 2.ä½œç”¨ï¼š

- æ•°æ®å˜ï¼Œè§†å›¾è·Ÿç€å˜ :value

## äº”äºŒã€è¡¨å•ç±»ç»„ä»¶å°è£…

```vue
            <option value="102">ä¸Šæµ·</option>
            <option value="103">æ­¦æ±‰</option>
```

## äº”å…­ã€å¼‚æ­¥æ›´æ–° & $nextTick

### 2.ä»£ç å®ç°

```vue

        <div v-if="isShowEdit">

        <div v-else>
            <span>{{ title }}</span>
            <button @click="editFn">ç¼–è¾‘</button>

    export default {
        data() {
            return {
                title: 'å¤§æ ‡é¢˜',
                isShowEdit: false,
                editValue: '',

            editFn() {
                // æ˜¾ç¤ºè¾“å…¥æ¡†
                this.isShowEdit = true
                // è·å–ç„¦ç‚¹
                this.$nextTick(() => this.$refs.inp.focus())

        },
    }
</script>
```

## äº”å…«ã€è‡ªå®šä¹‰æŒ‡ä»¤-æŒ‡ä»¤çš„å€¼

### 2.è¯­æ³•

```vue
                    el.style.color = bind.value
                }
            }
        }
    }
```

## äº”ä¹ã€è‡ªå®šä¹‰æŒ‡ä»¤-v-loadingæŒ‡ä»¤çš„å°è£…

### 1.åœºæ™¯

å®é™…å¼€å‘è¿‡ç¨‹ä¸­ï¼Œå‘é€è¯·æ±‚éœ€è¦æ—¶é—´ï¼Œåœ¨è¯·æ±‚çš„æ•°æ®æœªå›æ¥æ—¶ï¼Œé¡µé¢ä¼šå¤„äº**ç©ºç™½çŠ¶æ€**  =>  ç”¨æˆ·ä½“éªŒä¸å¥½

### 2.éœ€æ±‚

å°è£…ä¸€ä¸ª v-loading æŒ‡ä»¤ï¼Œå®ç°åŠ è½½ä¸­çš„æ•ˆæœ

### 3.åˆ†æ

1. æœ¬è´¨ loadingæ•ˆæœå°±æ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªè’™å±‚ï¼Œç›–åœ¨äº†ç›’å­ä¸Š
2. æ•°æ®è¯·æ±‚ä¸­ï¼Œå¼€å¯loadingçŠ¶æ€ï¼Œæ·»åŠ è’™å±‚
3. æ•°æ®è¯·æ±‚å®Œæ¯•ï¼Œå…³é—­loadingçŠ¶æ€ï¼Œç§»é™¤è’™å±‚

### 4.å®ç°

1. å‡†å¤‡ä¸€ä¸ª loadingç±»ï¼Œé€šè¿‡ä¼ªå…ƒç´ å®šä½ï¼Œè®¾ç½®å®½é«˜ï¼Œå®ç°è’™å±‚
2. å¼€å¯å…³é—­ loadingçŠ¶æ€ï¼ˆæ·»åŠ ç§»é™¤è’™å±‚ï¼‰ï¼Œæœ¬è´¨åªéœ€è¦æ·»åŠ ç§»é™¤ç±»å³å¯
3. ç»“åˆè‡ªå®šä¹‰æŒ‡ä»¤çš„è¯­æ³•è¿›è¡Œå°è£…å¤ç”¨

```css
.loading:before {
    content: "";
    position: absolute;
    left: 0;
    top: 0;
    width: 100%;
    height: 100%;
    background: #fff url("./loading.gif") no-repeat center;
```

### 5.å‡†å¤‡ä»£ç 

```html
<template>
    <div class="main">
        <div class="box" v-loading="isLoading">
            <ul>
                <li v-for="item in list" :key="item.id" class="news">
                    <div class="left">
                        <div class="title">{{ item.title }}</div>
                        <div class="info">
                            <span>{{ item.source }}</span>
                            <span>{{ item.time }}</span>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="right">
                        <img :src="item.img" alt="">
                    </div>
                </li>
            </ul>
        </div>
    </div>
</template>

<script>
    // å®‰è£…axios =>  yarn add axios || npm i axios
    import axios from 'axios'

    // æ¥å£åœ°å€ï¼šhttp://hmajax.itheima.net/api/news
    // è¯·æ±‚æ–¹å¼ï¼šget
    export default {
        data() {
            return {
                list: [],
                isLoading: true
            }
        },
        async created() {
            // 1. å‘é€è¯·æ±‚è·å–æ•°æ®
            const res = await axios.get('http://hmajax.itheima.net/api/news')

            setTimeout(() => {
                // 2. æ›´æ–°åˆ° list ä¸­ï¼Œç”¨äºé¡µé¢æ¸²æŸ“ v-for
                this.list = res.data.data
                this.isLoading = false
            }, 2000)
        },
        directives: {
            loading: {
                inserted(el, binding) {
                    if (binding.value) {
                        el.classList.add('loading')
                    }
                },
                update(el, binding) {
                    if (binding.value) {
                        el.classList.add('loading')
                    } else {
                        el.classList.remove('loading')
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
</script>

<style>
    .loading:before {
        content: '';
        position: absolute;
        left: 0;
        top: 0;
        width: 100%;
        height: 100%;
        background: #fff url('./loading.gif') no-repeat center;
    }

    .box2 {
        width: 400px;
        height: 400px;
        border: 2px solid #000;
        position: relative;
    }


    .box {
        width: 800px;
        min-height: 500px;
        border: 3px solid orange;
        border-radius: 5px;
        position: relative;
    }

    .news {
        display: flex;
        height: 120px;
        width: 600px;
        margin: 0 auto;
        padding: 20px 0;
        cursor: pointer;
    }

    .news .left {
        flex: 1;
        display: flex;
        flex-direction: column;
        justify-content: space-between;
        padding-right: 10px;
    }

    .news .left .title {
        font-size: 20px;
    }

    .news .left .info {
        color: #999999;
    }

    .news .left .info span {
        margin-right: 20px;
    }

    .news .right {
        width: 160px;
        height: 120px;
    }

    .news .right img {
        width: 100%;
        height: 100%;
        object-fit: cover;
    }
</style>
```

App.vue

```vue
<template>
    <div>
        <MyTable :data="list">
            <template #default="obj">
                <button @click="del(obj.row.id)">åˆ é™¤</button>
            </template>
        </MyTable>
        <MyTable :data="list2">
            <template #default="obj">
                <button @click="show(obj)">æŸ¥çœ‹</button>
            </template>
        </MyTable>
    </div>
</template>

<script>
import MyTable from './components/MyTable.vue'

export default {
    data() {
        return {
            list: [
                {id: 1, name: 'å¼ å°èŠ±', age: 18},
                {id: 2, name: 'å­™å¤§æ˜', age: 19},
                {id: 3, name: 'åˆ˜å¾·å¿ ', age: 17},
            ],
            list2: [
                {id: 1, name: 'èµµå°äº‘', age: 18},
                {id: 2, name: 'åˆ˜è““è““', age: 19},
                {id: 3, name: 'å§œè‚–æ³°', age: 17},
            ]
        }
    },
    components: {
        MyTable
    },
    methods: {
        del(id) {
            this.list = this.list.filter(ie => ie.id !== id)
        },
        show(obj) {
            console.log(`message is ${obj.msg}, id is ${obj.row.id}, name is ${obj.row.name}, age is ${obj.row.age}`)
        }
    }
}
</script>
```

## ä¹ä¸€ã€ESlintä»£ç è§„èŒƒåŠæ‰‹åŠ¨ä¿®å¤

ä»£ç è§„èŒƒï¼šä¸€å¥—å†™ä»£ç çš„çº¦å®šè§„åˆ™ã€‚ä¾‹å¦‚ï¼šèµ‹å€¼ç¬¦å·çš„å·¦å³æ˜¯å¦éœ€è¦ç©ºæ ¼ï¼Ÿä¸€å¥ç»“æŸæ˜¯å¦æ˜¯è¦åŠ `;`ï¼Ÿ...

>  æ²¡æœ‰è§„çŸ©ä¸æˆæ–¹åœ†

ESLintæ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªä»£ç æ£€æŸ¥å·¥å…·ï¼Œç”¨æ¥æ£€æŸ¥ä½ çš„ä»£ç æ˜¯å¦ç¬¦åˆæŒ‡å®šçš„è§„åˆ™(ä½ å’Œä½ çš„å›¢é˜Ÿå¯ä»¥è‡ªè¡Œçº¦å®šä¸€å¥—è§„åˆ™)ã€‚åœ¨åˆ›å»ºé¡¹ç›®æ—¶ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬ä½¿ç”¨çš„æ˜¯ [JavaScript Standard Style](https://standardjs.com/readme-zhcn.html) ä»£ç é£æ ¼çš„è§„åˆ™ã€‚

#### 1.JavaScript Standard Style è§„èŒƒè¯´æ˜

å»ºè®®æŠŠï¼šhttps://standardjs.com/rules-zhcn.html çœ‹ä¸€éï¼Œç„¶ååœ¨å†™çš„æ—¶å€™,  é‡åˆ°é”™è¯¯å°±æŸ¥è¯¢è§£å†³ã€‚

ä¸‹é¢æ˜¯è¿™ä»½è§„åˆ™ä¸­çš„ä¸€å°éƒ¨åˆ†ï¼š

- *å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ä½¿ç”¨å•å¼•å·* â€“ éœ€è¦è½¬ä¹‰çš„åœ°æ–¹é™¤å¤–
- *æ— åˆ†å·* â€“ [è¿™](http://blog.izs.me/post/2353458699/an-open-letter-to-javascript-leaders-regarding)[æ²¡ä»€ä¹ˆä¸å¥½ã€‚](http://inimino.org/~inimino/blog/javascript_semicolons)[ä¸éª—ä½ ï¼](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=gsfbh17Ax9I)
- *å…³é”®å­—ååŠ ç©ºæ ¼* `if (condition) { ... }`
- *å‡½æ•°åååŠ ç©ºæ ¼* `function name (arg) { ... }`
- åšæŒä½¿ç”¨å…¨ç­‰ `===` æ‘’å¼ƒ `==` ä¸€ä½†åœ¨éœ€è¦æ£€æŸ¥ `null || undefined` æ—¶å¯ä»¥ä½¿ç”¨ `obj == null`
- ......

#### 2.ä»£ç è§„èŒƒé”™è¯¯

å¦‚æœä½ çš„ä»£ç ä¸ç¬¦åˆstandardçš„è¦æ±‚ï¼Œeslintä¼šè·³å‡ºæ¥åˆ€å­å˜´ï¼Œè±†è…å¿ƒåœ°æç¤ºä½ ã€‚

ä¸‹é¢æˆ‘ä»¬åœ¨main.jsä¸­éšæ„åšä¸€äº›æ”¹åŠ¨ï¼šæ·»åŠ ä¸€äº›ç©ºè¡Œï¼Œç©ºæ ¼ã€‚

```js

import App from './App.vue'

import './styles/index.less'
import router from './router'

new Vue({
    render: h => h(App),
    router

```

æŒ‰ä¸‹ä¿å­˜ä»£ç ä¹‹åï¼š

ä½ å°†ä¼šçœ‹åœ¨æ§åˆ¶å°ä¸­è¾“å‡ºå¦‚ä¸‹é”™è¯¯ï¼š

![68294255431](assets/1682942554314.png)

> eslint æ˜¯æ¥å¸®åŠ©ä½ çš„ã€‚å¿ƒæ€è¦å¥½ï¼Œæœ‰é”™ï¼Œå°±æ”¹ã€‚

## ä¹ä¸ƒã€é€šè¿‡è¾…åŠ©å‡½æ•°  - mapStateè·å– stateä¸­çš„æ•°æ®

>mapStateæ˜¯è¾…åŠ©å‡½æ•°ï¼Œå¸®åŠ©æˆ‘ä»¬æŠŠstoreä¸­çš„æ•°æ®æ˜ å°„åˆ° ç»„ä»¶çš„è®¡ç®—å±æ€§ä¸­, å®ƒå±äºä¸€ç§æ–¹ä¾¿çš„ç”¨æ³•

## ä¹å…«ã€å¼€å¯ä¸¥æ ¼æ¨¡å¼åŠVuexçš„å•é¡¹æ•°æ®æµ

```vue
	 handleAdd (n) {
```

### 3.å¼€å¯ä¸¥æ ¼æ¨¡å¼

é€šè¿‡ `strict: true` å¯ä»¥å¼€å¯ä¸¥æ ¼æ¨¡å¼ï¼Œå¼€å¯ä¸¥æ ¼æ¨¡å¼åï¼Œç›´æ¥ä¿®æ”¹stateä¸­çš„å€¼ä¼šæŠ¥é”™

> **stateæ•°æ®çš„ä¿®æ”¹åªèƒ½é€šè¿‡mutationsï¼Œå¹¶ä¸”mutationså¿…é¡»æ˜¯åŒæ­¥çš„**

## ä¹ä¹ã€æ ¸å¿ƒæ¦‚å¿µ-mutations

### 1.å®šä¹‰mutations

```js
const store = new Vuex.Store({
    state: {
        count: 0
    },
    // å®šä¹‰mutations
    mutations: {}
})
```

### 2.æ ¼å¼è¯´æ˜

mutationsæ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªå¯¹è±¡ï¼Œå¯¹è±¡ä¸­å­˜æ”¾ä¿®æ”¹stateçš„æ–¹æ³•

```vue

    // æ–¹æ³•é‡Œå‚æ•° ç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªå‚æ•°æ˜¯å½“å‰storeçš„stateå±æ€§
    // payload è½½è· è¿è¾“å‚æ•° è°ƒç”¨mutaiionsçš„æ—¶å€™ å¯ä»¥ä¼ é€’å‚æ•° ä¼ é€’è½½è·
    addCount(state) {
        state.count += 1
    }
}
```

### 3.ç»„ä»¶ä¸­æäº¤ mutations

```jsx
this.$store.commit('addCount')
```

## ä¸€ç™¾ã€å¸¦å‚æ•°çš„ mutations

### 1.ç›®æ ‡ï¼š

æŒæ¡ mutations ä¼ å‚è¯­æ³•

### 2.è¯­æ³•

çœ‹ä¸‹é¢è¿™ä¸ªæ¡ˆä¾‹ï¼Œæ¯æ¬¡ç‚¹å‡»ä¸åŒçš„æŒ‰é’®ï¼ŒåŠ çš„å€¼éƒ½ä¸åŒï¼Œæ¯æ¬¡éƒ½è¦å®šä¹‰ä¸åŒçš„mutationså¤„ç†å—ï¼Ÿ

![68321700423](assets/1683217004239.png)

æäº¤ mutation æ˜¯å¯ä»¥ä¼ é€’å‚æ•°çš„ï¼š`this.$store.commit('xxx',  å‚æ•°)`

#### 2.1 æä¾›mutationå‡½æ•°ï¼ˆå¸¦å‚æ•°ï¼‰

```vue
mutations: {
    addCount(state, count) {
        state.count = count
    }
}
```

#### 2.2 æäº¤mutation

```vue
handle() {
    this.$store.commit('addCount', 10)
}
```

**å°tips: æäº¤çš„å‚æ•°åªèƒ½æ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ª, å¦‚æœæœ‰å¤šä¸ªå‚æ•°è¦ä¼ , å¯ä»¥ä¼ é€’ä¸€ä¸ªå¯¹è±¡**

```jsx
this.$store.commit('addCount', {
  count: 10
})
```

## ä¸€é›¶ä¸€ã€ç»ƒä¹ -mutationsçš„å‡æ³•åŠŸèƒ½

![68321724875](assets/1683217248752.png)

### 1.æ­¥éª¤

![68321726825](assets/1683217268256.png)

### 2.ä»£ç å®ç°

Son2.vue

```vue
<template>
    <button @click="subCount(1)">å€¼ - 1</button>
    <button @click="subCount(5)">å€¼ - 5</button>
    <button @click="subCount(10)">å€¼ - 10</button>
</template>

<script>
export default {
    methods: {
        subCount(n) {
            this.$store.commit('addCount', n)
        },
    }
}
</script>
```

store/index.js

```js
mutations:{
    subCount (state, n) {
      state.count -= n
    },
}
```

## ä¸€é›¶äºŒã€ç»ƒä¹ -Vuexä¸­çš„å€¼å’Œç»„ä»¶ä¸­çš„inputåŒå‘ç»‘å®š

### 1.ç›®æ ‡

å®æ—¶è¾“å…¥ï¼Œå®æ—¶æ›´æ–°ï¼Œå·©å›º mutations ä¼ å‚è¯­æ³•

![68321769706](assets/1683217697064.png)

### 2.å®ç°æ­¥éª¤

![68321771778](assets/1683217717788.png)

### 3.ä»£ç å®ç°

App.vue

```vue
<template>
    <input :value="count" @input="handleInput" type="text">
</template>

<script>
export default {
    methods: {
        handleInput(e) {
            // 1. å®æ—¶è·å–è¾“å…¥æ¡†çš„å€¼
            const num = +e.target.value
            // 2. æäº¤mutationï¼Œè°ƒç”¨mutationå‡½æ•°
            this.$store.commit('changeCount', num)
        }
    }
}
</script>
```

## ä¸€é›¶å››ã€æ ¸å¿ƒæ¦‚å¿µ - actions

> stateæ˜¯å­˜æ”¾æ•°æ®çš„ï¼Œmutationsæ˜¯åŒæ­¥æ›´æ–°æ•°æ® (ä¾¿äºç›‘æµ‹æ•°æ®çš„å˜åŒ–, æ›´æ–°è§†å›¾ç­‰, æ–¹ä¾¿äºè°ƒè¯•å·¥å…·æŸ¥çœ‹å˜åŒ–)ï¼Œ

## äºŒåä¸€ã€Vuexæ¨¡å—åŒ–çš„ä½¿ç”¨å°ç»“

2. ç»„ä»¶ä¸­ç›´æ¥ä½¿ç”¨ å±æ€§ `{{ age }}` æˆ– æ–¹æ³• `@click="updateAge(2)"`

## äºŒåäºŒã€ç»¼åˆæ¡ˆä¾‹ - åˆ›å»ºé¡¹ç›®

## äºŒåå››ã€ç»¼åˆæ¡ˆä¾‹-å‡†å¤‡åç«¯æ¥å£æœåŠ¡ç¯å¢ƒ(äº†è§£)

1. å®‰è£…å…¨å±€å·¥å…· json-server ï¼ˆå…¨å±€å·¥å…·ä»…éœ€è¦å®‰è£…ä¸€æ¬¡ï¼‰

## äºŒåäº”ã€ç»¼åˆæ¡ˆä¾‹-è¯·æ±‚åŠ¨æ€æ¸²æŸ“æ•°æ®

### 1.ç›®æ ‡

è¯·æ±‚è·å–æ•°æ®å­˜å…¥ vuex, æ˜ å°„æ¸²æŸ“

![68343647192](assets/1683436471929.png)

1. å®‰è£… axios

```jsx
yarn add axios
```

2. å‡†å¤‡actions å’Œ mutations

```jsx
import axios from 'axios'

export default {
  namespaced: true,
  state () {
    return {
      list: []
    }
  },
  mutations: {
    updateList (state, payload) {
      state.list = payload
    }
  },
  actions: {
    async getList (ctx) {
      const res = await axios.get('http://localhost:3000/cart')
      ctx.commit('updateList', res.data)
    }
  }
}
```

3. `App.vue`é¡µé¢ä¸­è°ƒç”¨ action,  è·å–æ•°æ®

```jsx
import { mapState } from 'vuex'

export default {
  name: 'App',
  components: {
    CartHeader,
    CartFooter,
    CartItem
  },
  created () {
    this.$store.dispatch('cart/getList')
  },
  computed: {
    ...mapState('cart', ['list'])
  }
}
```

4. åŠ¨æ€æ¸²æŸ“

```jsx
<!-- å•†å“ Item é¡¹ç»„ä»¶ -->
<cart-item v-for="item in list" :key="item.id" :item="item"></cart-item>
```

`cart-item.vue`

```jsx

    </div>
```

## äºŒåå…­ã€ç»¼åˆæ¡ˆä¾‹-ä¿®æ”¹æ•°é‡

![68343734699](assets/1683437346997.png)

1. æ³¨å†Œç‚¹å‡»äº‹ä»¶

```jsx
<!-- æŒ‰é’®åŒºåŸŸ -->
<button class="btn btn-light" @click="onBtnClick(-1)">-</button>
<span class="count">{{item.count}}</span>
<button class="btn btn-light" @click="onBtnClick(1)">+</button>
```

2. é¡µé¢ä¸­dispatch action

```jsx
onBtnClick (step) {
  const newCount = this.item.count + step
  if (newCount < 1) return

  // å‘é€ä¿®æ”¹æ•°é‡è¯·æ±‚
  this.$store.dispatch('cart/updateCount', {
    id: this.item.id,
    count: newCount
  })
}
```

3. æä¾›actionå‡½æ•°

```jsx
async updateCount (ctx, payload) {
  await axios.patch('http://localhost:3000/cart/' + payload.id, {
    count: payload.count
  })
  ctx.commit('updateCount', payload)
}
```

4. æä¾›mutationå¤„ç†å‡½æ•°

```jsx
mutations: {
  ...,
  updateCount (state, payload) {
    const goods = state.list.find((item) => item.id === payload.id)
    goods.count = payload.count
  }
},
```



## äºŒåä¸ƒã€ç»¼åˆæ¡ˆä¾‹-åº•éƒ¨æ€»ä»·å±•ç¤º

1. æä¾›getters

```jsx
getters: {
  total(state) {
    return state.list.reduce((p, c) => p + c.count, 0);
  },
  totalPrice (state) {
    return state.list.reduce((p, c) => p + c.count * c.price, 0);
  },
},
```

2. åŠ¨æ€æ¸²æŸ“

```jsx
<template>
  <div class="footer-container">
    <!-- ä¸­é—´çš„åˆè®¡ -->
    <div>
      <span>å…± {{total}} ä»¶å•†å“ï¼Œåˆè®¡ï¼š</span>
      <span class="price">ï¿¥{{totalPrice}}</span>
    </div>
    <!-- å³ä¾§ç»“ç®—æŒ‰é’® -->
    <button class="btn btn-success btn-settle">ç»“ç®—</button>
  </div>
</template>

<script>
import { mapGetters } from 'vuex'
export default {
  name: 'CartFooter',
  computed: {
    ...mapGetters('cart', ['total', 'totalPrice'])
  }
}
</script>
```
